Important News II

Mayor of Beijing, Wei Daoming, Assumes Office 48

The newly appointed Mayor of Nanjing Special Municipality, Wei Daoming, arrived at the municipal government yesterday (the 19th) at 10:00 AM to assume his duties. Former Mayor Liu Jiwen convened a meeting with all staff in the main auditorium at 9:00 AM. The details are recorded separately below:

Yesterday at 9:00 AM, former Mayor Liu Jiwen convened a meeting with all staff in the main auditorium to deliver his final farewell remarks. Apart from the heads of the various bureaus, approximately 200 people were present. Mr. Liu briefly stated: "Since I was appointed to resume my post as Mayor of Beijing in July of the 17th year of the Republic [1928], it has been one year and nine months. During this period, I have not seen any significant achievements that could satisfy the citizens, and I feel very sorry. Therefore, I am eager to leave, hoping that my successor can gradually make improvements and complete the construction plan. What I want to say today is: (1) The waterworks project has been completed and is expected to be finished by the end of the 20th year of the Republic [1931], which will solve the drinking water problem for the citizens. (2) The establishment of the Municipal Bank has facilitated the financial circulation of the city and can provide emergency relief to the poor. The bank's credit is now very reliable, which is a welcome phenomenon. (3) The preparation of the Municipal Library is only in its rudimentary form, and the central government has agreed to allocate funds to subsidize municipal primary education, which will greatly benefit citizen education in the future. I hope that the new Mayor Wei will continue to advance these points and complete them to fulfill the original intention. I am about to go to Shanghai, and I feel very attached to you all at this parting. I am now giving you my final farewell, and I hope you will work hard. Please take care." After Liu Jiwen finished speaking, the new mayor had not yet arrived, so he rested in the mayor's office. About 20 minutes later, the new Mayor Wei Daoming arrived in the same car with Ma Shouhua, the Chief Secretary of the Ministry of Judicial Administration. When they arrived in front of the auditorium, the military band played music, and all the staff stood up to welcome them. After Wei got out of the car, he went to the mayor's office to meet Liu Jiwen for a brief exchange. Wei's receiving personnel, Wang Zuyi, Chen Haitao, Qi Xu, and others, eight in total, arrived at the municipal government. All documents from the secretariat and the councilor's office were checked and handed over by Secretary-General Qian Hong, Zhang Xifan, Yu Xijiu, and others. At 10:15 AM, Liu Jiwen said goodbye, and Wei Daoming saw him off to the office door. When Liu left the auditorium, all the staff stood up to see him off. Liu nodded and left hurriedly.

After Liu Jiwen left, the new Mayor Wei Daoming went to the auditorium and addressed all the staff, saying: "Fellow comrades, I have come here today very hastily. Because in the past few days, on the one hand, I have been dealing with the affairs of the Ministry of Judicial Administration and handing over my responsibilities, and on the other hand, I have had to attend the plenary session of the Capital Construction Committee. And Mayor Liu is about to go to Shanghai to take up his new post. Therefore, I have not yet had the time to study the actual situation of the city in detail. I cannot immediately report a specific plan on how to promote municipal administration in the future. However, I do have one feeling, which is that when the Capital Construction Committee met a few days ago, everyone believed that building the capital was extremely important and urgent. Although there are many difficulties and it is not easy to handle, everyone can work harder to achieve it. Municipal construction is of great importance, with the central government entrusting us with great responsibility and the citizens of the capital placing high expectations on us. We can only use the spirit of revolution, scientific methods, and collective efforts to jointly promote the development of municipal administration. You have been serving here for many years, helping Mayor Liu do a lot of work in the midst of hardship and difficulty. I am very impressed and still hope that you will help me do things with the spirit of helping Mayor Liu. We will have many opportunities to talk in the future, and we will talk more about it another day." After Wei finished speaking, a reporter from the Central News Agency interviewed him in the mayor's office, asking for his opinions on the city's municipal administration. Wei said, "Recently, I have been quite busy attending the plenary session of the Capital Construction Committee and handling the handover of affairs at the Ministry of Judicial Administration. I came here hastily today to assume my duties, but first, I will complete the internal handover and then gradually reorganize things. I will discuss long-term and great municipal construction plans in the long run to seek perfection and strive to achieve perfect results. Moreover, construction requires long-term hard work to be effective. In the future, I hope that the citizens will help the government in everything to achieve the effect of cooperation between officials and the people." As for the heads of the various bureaus under the municipal government, they had previously resigned from Liu Jiwen one after another to prepare for the handover. The candidates for the successors are said to have been internally determined: Zhu Baorou as the Director of the Education Bureau, Li Zongkan as the Director of the Public Works Bureau, Liang Weisi as the Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, Kong Xiankeng as the Director of the Land Bureau, Ma Shouhua as the Secretary-General, and a Mr. Li as the Director of the Health Bureau. They are expected to be announced in the next few days.

Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance Implements Austerity Plan 49

▲Abolish Finance Bureaus in Seventeen Counties

▲Rectify Provincial Tax Collection Agencies

Since the reorganization of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, Chairman Ye Chucang and the provincial committee members, in view of the excessive difference between the province's financial revenue and expenditure, have decided to reduce the originally planned recurring expenses of the various departments and affiliated institutions, which has been approved and implemented by the last provincial government meeting. Recently, Chen Qicai, Director of the Department of Finance, based on the newly determined budget, found that the provincial revenue was still more than 2 million short each year. He proposed to abolish the two bureaus of Finance and Construction in the Xuzhou and Haizhou areas, as well as the agricultural and forestry farms, and return them to the county governments for concurrent management, in order to save expenses. After consultation among the provincial committee members, it was decided to abolish the finance bureaus in seventeen counties, including Tongshan, Fengxian, Peixian, Xiaoxian, Dangshan, Pixian, Suqian, Qiaoning, Donghai, Ganyu, Shutang, Guanyun, Chongming, Qidong, Huaiyin, Lianshui, and Yangzhong (Note: Only deputy directors were previously established in the twelve counties of Tongshan, etc., with the county magistrates concurrently serving as the directors; in the five counties of Chongming, etc., both directors and deputy directors were established). Whether to abolish the Bureau of Construction will be decided after the Department of Construction discusses it. The agricultural and forestry farms will be decided when the new budget for the nineteenth year is prepared. However, if the newly organized Security Department of Jiangsu Province is implemented according to the current proposed plan, it should require more than 2 million in annual expenses, but there is no guarantee of the source of funds. Therefore, they are currently discussing a win-win solution. In addition, Chen believes that the clearing up of tax collection agencies in Jiangsu Province seems to be inferior to Zhejiang, and he is now actively trying to rectify them in order to increase tax revenue (Riri News Agency).

Telegrams Regarding the Resolution of the Gao Bu Affair in Zhucheng 50

▲Gao Guizi Still Supports the Central Government

Jinan Dispatch: Gao Guizi's troops have been transferred from Zhucheng and Juxian to Tai'an and placed under the command of Ma Hongkui. However, Gao's troops requested to set off two weeks after the siege was lifted. Chen Tiaoyuan ordered them to set off three days after being disarmed. Ma Hongkui sent Councilor Cao Jiqing to Juxian to discuss the matter with Gao, but he has not yet returned. Representatives from Zhucheng, Zhang Yan, and representatives from Juxian, Meng Ming, went to the provincial government yesterday to meet with Chairman Chen, requesting a quick lifting of the siege. Chen sent Adjutant Bai Yushan to tell the representatives to wait quietly for two or three days for a resolution. The reason for the resolution is that Gao Guizi sent a telegram to Commander-in-Chief Jiang, stating that he was still willing to be loyal to the country. Commander-in-Chief Jiang replied in approval, and Ma Fuxiang mediated. Jiang Huiruo, Cao Jiqing, Guo Nianzhen, and others also traveled back and forth. The incoming and outgoing telegrams from all parties are recorded below:

▲Gao Guizi's Telegram to Commander-in-Chief Jiang: Nanjing Commander-in-Chief Jiang Junjian, Secret, Councilor Guo Nianzhen came to Juxian to announce your instructions. All officers and soldiers are grateful for your kindness. The troops under my command are stationed in Shandong, suppressing bandits and pacifying the people, fulfilling their natural duties. The previous Zhucao Incident was unclear, and I believe that you have insight into the rights and wrongs. Now that the party and the country are in trouble, and we are revolutionary soldiers, we should support the central government and strive for early unification. Commander-in-Chief Ma Hongkui has moved his troops to Shandong, which is a major mission. I am willing to have my troops listen to his command. If there is anything inappropriate, please instruct us to follow. Respectfully, Gao Guizi.

▲Commander-in-Chief Jiang's Telegram to Gao Guizi: Juxian Division Commander Gao Peiwu, Secret, Your winter telegram has been read. You are a revolutionary soldier with meritorious service. I am very pleased that you have requested to lead your troops to support the central government and return to Commander-in-Chief Ma. It should be approved and handled. In addition to sending separate telegrams, I hope you will contact Commander-in-Chief Ma to handle it and wait for further instructions. Jiang Zhongzheng.

▲Ma Fuxiang's Telegram to Two Representatives: Nanjing Juxian Please forward to Councilor Jiang Huiruo Councilor Cao Jiqing, Secret, Your telegram has been read. I am very pleased that Gao's troops are willing to be loyal to the central government. The proposed methods are also very appropriate and have been presented to the President for review, who agrees. The President is going to Xuzhou today, and Xiang has also telegraphed Hongkui, instructing him to ask for instructions nearby. Please tell Division Commander Gao not to lose heart and continue to lead his troops to serve the country. Xiang's efforts will be sincere. I just talked to the director of the division's office in Beijing, and we had a very pleasant conversation. I also instructed him to telegraph Peiwu. Ma Fuxiang.

▲Lin Wei's Telegram to Guo Nianzhen: Councilor Guo Nianzhen, Your telegram has been read. Secret, The Gao Division's problem will be resolved soon. You should wait for the case to be closed before waiting for the President's telegram to handle it. Lin Wei.

Wuhu Quick News 51

▲The Wuhu People's Food Maintenance Association convened a meeting today at the General Chamber of Commerce, inviting various organizations and public groups to discuss the food problem. It was generally agreed that the Executive Yuan's resolution to prohibit the export of rice from Wuhu has brought the food situation in Wuhu to an extremely dangerous stage. The total amount of rice stored in Wuhu is only about 30,000 piculs, which is not enough to maintain the city's food supply for half a month. As a result, it was decided that all sectors would jointly send a telegram to the National Government, stating that it would be impossible to lift the ban on rice exports from Wuhu. At the same time, they would telegraph the provincial government, requesting that it issue an order to allow the circulation of rice and grain within the province. In order to provide relief to the poor, nine organizations, including the municipal and county party headquarters, the municipal government, and the General Chamber of Commerce, were tasked with discussing solutions for implementing price stabilization measures.

▲Lu Xueshu, the Commander of the Capital Garrison Regiment, recently led his troops from Wuhu to Fanchang to suppress bandits. They killed more than 40 bandits and seized 34 firearms. Lu returned to Wuhu from Fanchang today and is expected to go to Fanchang again within the next few days to eliminate the remaining bandits. All captured bandits will be sent to Wuhu for interrogation.

▲The Municipal Public Security Bureau, acting on the order of the Provincial Party Headquarters, arrested eight reactionary young men and seized multiple pieces of evidence near the Sanmei Temple at 11:00 PM last night. They are currently being secretly interrogated.

▲The General Headquarters previously sent personnel to Wuhu to purchase 50,000 piculs of military rice, but only 5,000 piculs have been purchased and transported to Beijing. Recently, due to the very low rice reserves in Wuhu, they have turned to Xuancheng, Nanling, and other places to purchase rice and have requested the Wuhu Garrison Regiment to send troops to escort the transportation. (18th)

Local dispatches

Jiading 52

Jiading-Xiang Lun Changes Timetable: The Jinghu Railway connecting Jiading and Nanxiang's commuter boats have added train services to the Jinghu Railway and changed the driving schedule. The ship will also increase flights and change the connecting time with the train, starting on the 20th.

Guns and Bullets Found Under Coffin: Near Gujiazhai, Yangdian Township, Waigang, there is a coffin that has not been buried. On the 16th of this month, a farmer, Farmer A, discovered 55 Mauser bullets for the Ninth Xiang Rifle under the coffin while working in the fields. The farmer reported to the district office. Director Fu sent the Home Guard to the village to investigate, but no other items were found. According to the farmers in the area, half a month ago, in the middle of the night, non-locals formed a team and blew police whistles to scare the farmers. Later, the local farmers fired shotguns to demonstrate and drove them away. This area is located at the intersection of Kunshan, Qingpu, and Jiading counties. Weapons such as hidden firearms were found in previous years.

Two Cases of Unidentified Male Corpses Discovered: An unidentified male corpse was found floating in Huanggu Pond in Beixiang. The acting district chief of the district reported to the county and sent officials to verify the matter. The corpse was wearing short clothes and was about 50 years old. There were no injuries. He drowned in the river. No family members were found. The district office prepared a coffin and buried him. Also, an unidentified male corpse was found floating in the Hengli River in Nanxiang. The police in Malu Township reported to the county and sent personnel to examine the body. The examination revealed that the corpse had been dead for many days. The corpse was rotten and could not be identified. Stones were tied to both feet with ropes, and it was suspected that he was murdered and thrown into the river. No family members were found. The township police were ordered to put the corpse in a coffin and bury it, and report back to the county government for verification.

Qingpu 53

Record of Court Hearing on Case of Party Committee Beating: Qingpu County's Fourth District Party Headquarters Standing Committee.

The County Government held a court hearing on the afternoon of the day before yesterday at 3:00 PM. The plaintiff, Dai Diren, was interrogated first. According to his statement, he is 24 years old, from Huangdu, and works in party affairs. On March 31, at 4:00 PM, he went to the Fenglinbang Elementary School with friends Pan Zhitao, Xie Fuhai, Gu Baoyu, and others to pay their respects. (Judge) How did Xu Amao, Yu Jinsheng, and others know that you threw away the lottery tube in the temple? (Answer) After I threw away the lottery tube, we went back to Huangdu. After walking about a mile, more than a dozen people chased after us, shouting to catch thieves. We were stopped by them and had to go back to the temple. They beat me. (Judge) Which people beat you? (Answer) Xu Amao, Yu Furong, and Yu Jinsheng were the most violent. They tied me up and beat me. Ding Jingfu, Ding Gengsheng, and A Xiangfu also hit me. The interrogating official then interrogated Xu Amao, who stated that he was 37 years old, from Qiujiaojiao, and worked as a tailor. (Question) When did Dai Diren throw away the lottery tube in front of the Bodhisattva? (Answer) On the 31st. (Question) After the lottery tube was thrown away, Dai Diren and others left. How did they come back to the temple? (Answer) I don't know. (Question) Did you tie up Dai Diren? (Answer) No. The interrogating official then interrogated Yu Jinsheng, who stated that he was 23 years old, from Fenglinbang, and sheared sheep. (Question) Who threw away the lottery tube in the Fenglinbang temple? (Answer) Dai Diren threw it away. (Question) Did you see him throw away the lottery tube? (Answer) No. (Question) You only went to chase him back after Dai Diren left the temple for more than a mile? (Answer) I didn't go to chase him. The interrogating official then ordered Xu Amao and Yu Jinsheng to be remanded in custody and ordered officials to verify the injuries suffered by Dai Diren, fill out a form and attach it to the file, and call in witnesses to testify and verify the matter.

Suzhou 54

Confession of Bandit Leader Tian Kuazi: Henan bandit leader Tian Kuazi was arrested on Jin Shenfu Road in Shanghai and is currently being held at the Garrison Headquarters. It is said that the bandit admitted that Mao Zilong, Zhang Zhaohua, Zheng Handa, and others gathered to loot Xueyanqiao, Luxu, Wuzhen, and resisted arrest in Xigang, killing Li Guobin, the captain of the Water Police Guerrilla. They were all present. Later, on the first day of the Lunar New Year, he separated from Mao and came to Shanghai from Zhejiang only a week ago. The gang's firearms are scattered and hidden in certain villages. However, according to another source, Tian came to Shanghai this time under the dispatch of Zheng Handa, who recently captured Si'an, and with accomplices Liang Pikui, Kong Kuazi, and others, prepared to contact the Haizhou gang. Unexpectedly, Zhang Zhaohua's gang in Haizhou had been wiped out in Yangcheng Lake.

Change of Trial Official in Jinshan County: The High Court announced that Peng Shen, the trial official of Jinshan County, would be reassigned, and Liu Chengkan would be temporarily appointed to fill the vacancy.

Order for Counties to Handle Bandit Suppression Vessels: The General Headquarters sent troops to suppress lake bandits, initially designating the seven counties along Taihu Lake, such as Suzhou, Changzhou, Changhu, etc., in Jiangsu and Zhejiang as bandit suppression areas. The troop strength was stipulated as the 25th and 30th regiments of the 5th Division. Later, with the approval of the Suzhou Provincial Government's request, troops were dispatched to search and suppress the two lakes of Yangcheng and Dianshan on the border of Suzhou and Kunshan, as well as Jinshan, Songjiang, and Qingpu counties. Hu, the Commander-in-Chief, ordered the 28th regiment stationed in Kunshan and the 3rd Battalion of the 26th regiment stationed in Songjiang, Qingpu, and Jinshan to dispatch troops to suppress bandits starting from the first day of this month. Recently, Hu telegraphed the Suzhou Provincial Government to allocate the bandit suppression expenses of the above-mentioned troops and requested that the four county governments of Kunshan, Jinshan, Songjiang, and Qingpu be instructed to handle the vehicles and ships needed for bandit suppression according to the Bandit Suppression Plan Outline promulgated by the General Headquarters. The Suzhou Provincial Government replied yesterday (the 20th) that it would handle the matter accordingly.

Changzhou 55

Enthusiasm for Promoting Domestic Goods Movement: The Propaganda Committee of the Wuyi County Party Rectification Association convened a meeting on the 19th, inviting people from all walks of life to promote the domestic goods movement. In the morning, a mass meeting was held in the public sports field, attended by five or six thousand people. There were impassioned speeches at the time. In the afternoon, a recreational show was held at the Mingxing Theater, with various agencies, groups, and schools performing. It was very lively. In the evening, a lantern parade was held, with various lanterns, military bands, etc., stretching for about three or four li. However, the weather was not good, and a thunderstorm suddenly occurred halfway through, so everyone had to disperse.

Bandit Arrested in the Western Suburbs: Robberies have repeatedly occurred in the Sanbao Township Haizhekou area of the western suburbs of Wuyi. Recently, a villager received a threatening letter demanding 500 yuan. Cui Siping, the patrolling officer of the Second Detachment of the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau, discovered that the bandit involved in the case, Wei Xiaopinzi, made a living by rowing wooden rafts and lived near the Tianhou Palace. He was arrested on the 19th and is scheduled to be sent to the County Court for interrogation on the 20th.

Zhenjiang 56

Department of Construction Sends Personnel to Inspect Route: Sun, the Director of the Department of Construction of Jiangsu Province, in order to inspect the route along Jiangyin, Wujin, Wuxi, Changshu, and Jiading, specially sent Xu Yihang, a technician from the Department, to inspect the matters of conscripting labor and building roads along the way in the respective counties. He also ordered the governments of the counties along the way to provide proper protection.

Foreigner Inquires About Tax Revenue, Department Orders Refusal: Oden, the American Consul in Beijing, sent an official letter to the Zhenjiang County Government the other day, stating that the office was planning to collect the types of taxes in its jurisdiction for statistical purposes and requested that the names of various taxes within the jurisdiction of Zhenjiang County and their tax rates be investigated and listed separately. After receiving the letter, County Magistrate Zhang believed that since China was seeking autonomy in tariffs, it seemed inappropriate for foreigners to inquire about local taxes. The reason for the consul's statistics was unknown. The types of taxes belonging to the county's income were still available for reference at the County Finance Bureau. As for the province's income, it could not be clarified without the instructions of the Department of Finance. He did not dare to decide whether to investigate and reply on his own and specially asked the Department of Finance for its approval and instructions. After receiving the report, Chen, the Director of the Department of Finance, believed that local taxes were entirely a matter of internal affairs and should not be asked about by foreigners. He specially instructed the Zhenjiang County Magistrate to politely decline with the excuse that it was inconvenient to disclose them without the order of the central government.

Yangzhou 57

Both Civil and Criminal Parts of the Zhu Jingwen Case Resolved: After repeated summons of witnesses by the County Government and court hearings, the criminal part of the Zhu Jingwen suicide case resulted in a sentence of one year imprisonment for Xu Zhicang (i.e., Zhu Jingwen's husband), which was commuted to two years probation. As for the other part, the private lawsuit for dowry compensation, Wang Jingting, Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, traveled back and forth between Yangzhou and Shanghai and mediated in many ways. As a result, Xu did not appeal in the criminal aspect, and Zhu asked for concessions in the civil aspect. It is now said that Zhu has agreed. As for the various lively activities requested by Zhu, such as Xu's chanting of scriptures and holding a memorial service, it is said that Xu will also do so.

Education Sector Strike on the Third Day: Due to a lack of funds, the education sector in Jiangdu has suspended teaching for three days. It is now said that County Magistrate Chen has agreed that once classes are resumed, the county will be responsible for issuing half a month's salary first (about 9,000 yuan). However, some teachers and staff advocate restoring the status quo immediately, while others insist that classes will not be held unless one and a half months of expenses are issued at the same time. It is now said that half of the classes are expected to resume next Monday.

Xiao Yufeng After the Closure of Yongjiheng: The sudden closure of the Yongjiheng Salt Store opened by Yun Merchant Zhou Weibin has had a considerable impact on the financial community in Yangzhou. Later, Wang Jingting, the representative of the Chamber of Commerce, went to Shanghai and negotiated repeatedly with Zhou's representative, Lawyer Luo, but to no avail. It is now said that the various money shops in Yangzhou that have dealings with the store intend to formally sue it, which has also involved the various salt stores opened by Xiao Yufeng, with rumors of closing half of them. As for the funds of the Shanghai financial community that have dealings with the various money shops in Yangzhou, Wang Jingting explained the situation in Shanghai, and the money will not be recovered for the time being. However, it is not easy to release another layer before the Zhou affair is resolved.

Planned Construction of Martyrs' Cemetery: Wang Boling, a member of the Provincial Government, issued a circular for the construction of the Xiong Martyrs' Cemetery, stating that he had raised more than 30,000 yuan from the national and provincial governments and the gentry and merchants of Yangzhou for the construction of the Xiong Martyrs' Cemetery, which was nearly half of the original plan of 30,000 yuan. In addition to continuing to solicit donations from all parties, a founding meeting will be held at the Xiaohua Garden in the south of the city on the 26th to discuss the progress and determine the location of the cemetery. The matter concerns the commendation of martyrs, and it is hoped that everyone will take the time to attend.

Inspector Goes to the Capital and is Promoted to Regiment Commander: Wang Yumen, the inspector of the Public Security Bureau, was summoned to the capital by Qin Qinglin, the Commander of the Provisional 4th Division, and was appointed as the Commander of the 2nd Regiment of the 2nd Brigade of the Division. Wang Zhui, Yin Rucheng, and Wang Mingzhong were appointed as the commanders of the 1st, 2nd, and 3rd Battalions of the Regiment. It is said that Wang is an old subordinate of Qin and will go to the front lines soon.

Limited Time for Completion of the Yanghuo Road Project: The Yanghuo Road project has not yet been completed. The county has specially instructed the Construction Bureau and the Second Autonomous District Office, as well as the general and branch leaders of the road, to fill in the road surface with earthwork and implement ramming and rolling within a week after the weather clears to ensure that it is solid. Dong Hengjin and other five people were jointly appointed by the Construction Bureau as eight section leaders, Wang Dongzhen and other four people as twelve and three section leaders, Wang Fenglu and other four people as eleven section leaders, Zhou Mingfu as seven section leader, and Tan Deyi and other five people as six section leaders to supervise the work.

Department Commits to Investigating Lawsuits: Chen Jianming, an inspector from the Department of Civil Affairs, came to Cheng the day before yesterday to investigate. What Will Be the Use of Privately Engraved Wooden Stamps?: Wang Yingen, a patrolling officer stationed at the Third Police Station of the Public Security Bureau, saw Xu Deming, a carving shop in Yuerong Alley, carving a square wooden stamp of the Garrison Commander the day before yesterday. Because the matter was abnormal, after questioning, it was said that it was carved by Wu Huijun, a partner of the Zhenhua Cloth Factory. Patrol Officer Wang reported to Director Dong and summoned Wu to the General Bureau. Director Zhang interrogated him. Wu confessed that he met a friend Xu Lu on the way, who was from Yixing and served as a special agent in the Nantong Police Brigade, and ordered him to carve it. He really did not know what it was for. After the interrogation, he was sent to the Department Government yesterday for questioning and was ordered to be detained pending judgment.

The court ruled on the first day of this month that Li Chengmin, Wang Tingyi, Wang Wenru, and other three people were innocent. The judgment was delivered on the fourth day. Now that the appeal period has expired, they will be released soon. The Jiangyin County Party Department convened a joint meeting of various agencies on the 18th to discuss measures and decided on the Zhou case. (Objectives of the Solution) (1) Punish the ringleaders and accomplices separately; (2) Provide preferential compensation; (3) Confiscate the property of the main criminals in the Zhou case as a fund for the Farmers Bank. (Decision-making methods) (1) Various agencies and groups will jointly present to the superior level and forward them to the High Court to handle the matter according to the objectives; (2) Restore the Zhou Case Investigation Committee to investigate the ringleaders and accomplices.

Bandits Rampant in Shuangpai Township: The houses of Gu Ruquan and Gu Youlang in Gujia Village, Shuangpai Township, east of the city, were burned down by bandits the night before last. The entire village of Zhanggujing Village was searched by bandits. None of the more than 20 households were spared. The bandits are very powerful.

Nantong 59

Requesting Relief for Overpayment of Provincial Taxes: The annual provincial tax collection in Tongyi is more than 130,000 yuan, and the payment of funds requires more than 210,000 yuan. At the moment, the Finance Bureau cannot cope and has submitted a request to the Department of Finance for relief.

County Magistrate's Resignation Approved: The resignation of Chen Buchan, the County Magistrate of Nantong, has been approved. The Provincial Government has appointed Zhang Dong to act on his behalf in Tong.

All Sectors Appeal for Delay in Transferring Provincial Police Team: The First Brigade of the Provincial Police Team is suppressing bandits in the eastern township and is currently searching the Caopengzhen area. It suddenly received an order from the province to transfer to Siyang. On the 19th, various sectors of the local community held a meeting and decided to petition the Provincial Department and the General Captain to postpone the transfer.

Customs No Longer Inspecting and Releasing Ocean Rice Transported to Tong: A rice shortage has occurred in Tongyi. At the moment, the local community is raising funds to purchase ocean rice and transport it back for relief. On the 19th, the Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs ordered the Nantong County Government that in the past two months, the county has handled more than 20,000 piculs of Shanghai rice, which should be sufficient for relief. Now that rice prices in Shanghai have soared, it is necessary to consider both sides. In the future, the inspection and release will be temporarily suspended, or it will be ordered to go to other places to purchase it. As the rice shortage is urgent here, the County Government should telegraph the Jianghai Customs to approve the inspection and release to maintain the people's food supply.

Qingjiang 60

Negotiating Joint Defense Measures for Two Counties: Zhao Zhenhua, Deputy Captain of the Huaiyin Police Force and concurrently Director of the Public Security Bureau, went to Siyang because banditry there was particularly rampant, making it almost impossible for the people to live in peace. Furthermore, the National Army stationed in Siyang, including the battalions of Xie Bingyan, Fu Zuoxiang, and Chen Weidong, had received orders to move and gather in Xin'an Town. Should banditry break out in Siyang in the future, the Huaiyin border areas such as Songji, Xuliu, and Wangwei, which border Siyang, would likely be affected. Therefore, on the 16th, he took a car to Si County to discuss joint defense measures for the two counties with County Magistrate Zhang Hongzhu and Public Security Bureau Director Xu Xinyou.

Capturing Bandits Who Attacked Pizhuang: On January 29th of this year, at dawn, a band of over a hundred bandits suddenly arrived at Pijiazhuang in the Fifth District of Huaiyin, breached the village defenses, and looted all the property, including cattle and donkeys. They also kidnapped fifty-one villagers. Although twenty-eight people were released on the evening of the same day, twenty-three people were still held for ransom. When the money was not received in time, Xu Huaizheng, one of the hostages, was shot dead as a warning. Subsequently, a total of over 1,700 silver dollars were extorted before the remaining twenty-two people were released one after another. Lu Zhongxian, Captain of the Second Squad of the Fifth District Police stationed in the county, recently reported that a bandit named Feng Yuyuan was involved in the case. Feng was arrested on the 13th, and confessed under interrogation. He also implicated Pi Renshan and Pi Chunshan, who were also arrested and sent to the brigade headquarters. After questioning by Brigade Commander Zhao, they were handed over to the county government for legal proceedings.

Rugao 61

Detailed Account of the Suppression of Bandits at Laohuzhuang: At around 10:00 AM on the 16th, a large band of four to five hundred bandits suddenly attacked Laohuzhuang in the Moshu District from four directions, setting fire to straw stacks along the way. Sun Xudong, the squad leader of the county police stationed in the village, led his troops and the militia to meet the attack from different directions. After three hours of fierce fighting, Squad Leader Sun held his ground, awaiting reinforcements. Subsequently, the militia from the Cheshi and Maping Wuyao districts, as well as the police from Kuang Shiying's First Squad, arrived to provide assistance. The bandits still resisted stubbornly. While the two sides were locked in a stalemate, Tang Dongru, the squad leader of the Tang Squad, arrived with his troops upon hearing the news, and joined the battle. The attack intensified. The bandits even used machine guns to strafe our troops, but before the bullets could be fired, the bandit holding the gun was shot and killed. The bandits then retreated westward. At this time, it was already 1:00 PM. In this battle, twenty to thirty bandits were killed and Zhu Yeying was captured alive. One light machine gun, one rifle, one pistol, one native cannon, one shoulder-fired gun, and one native gun were seized. The notorious criminal Shen Erhu and five other vicious bandits were beheaded and their heads were displayed on the four gates of the city as a warning to the public. Three soldiers from Sun's squad, Li Jiazan, Wang Yulin, and Sun Zhanliang, sustained minor injuries and have been sent to the hospital for treatment.

Brief News: (1) The county government has newly purchased 139 rifles and 69,500 rounds of ammunition, which were transported to Rugao yesterday. (2) The Rugao Housheng Store received 1,500 bags of Saigon rice from Shanghai yesterday. (3) The sixth district in the southwest of the county has suffered repeated banditry and the harvest has been poor, causing food shortages and panic among the people. The county party headquarters and the county government have jointly sent a telegram to the provincial government requesting funds for disaster relief. (4) The Department of Civil Affairs has ordered the county to impartially investigate the case in which Rugao tenant farmer representatives Niu Xilin and others accused Liu Changyan of colluding with local thugs to fabricate charges.

Huzhou 62

Situation After the Military and Police Recaptured Si'an: Although Changxing Si'an Town suffered no major losses after being occupied by bandits for twenty hours, five residents died. One was a carpenter, one was a flower carver, one was a young girl from a paper shop, one was a farmer, and one was a Henan person. All of the deceased were injured by stray bullets during the fighting. Afterwards, Regiment Commander Hang and the National Army battalion commanders Feng and Lai jointly issued a notice to merchants and residents to resume business as usual. The National Army and the security forces were stationed in the town, and the 11th Water Police Team was dispatched to defend Lincheng Bridge and Hongxing Bridge. Patrol Team Leader Yu was responsible for security. After the bandits withdrew from Si'an, they dispersed and fled towards Guangde, Anji, Changqiao Pass, and Dawu Mountain. Therefore, when Patrol Team Leader Yu arrived at Hongxing Bridge, he heard that over two hundred bandits had fled from Si'an and were hiding in Qianzi Village near Dawu Mountain. The team leader led his team to Dawu Mountain this morning to suppress the bandits.

County-Wide Police Conference: The newly appointed County Magistrate Shen Guangxiong, since assuming office, has paid special attention to defense. Furthermore, since the communists near Li Ze Yaozhuang Bridge have occasionally taken extreme actions, he specifically ordered all Public Security Bureau and police substation inspectors to hold a county-wide police conference in the county government hall the day before yesterday (the 16th). Several detailed rules for bandit prevention were discussed in order to ensure joint defense.

Bundling of Kidnapping Cases: The widow of Xu Xiangqing from Baimao River in Xitang, who was living with an old woman in a dilapidated house, was discovered by bandits. Last night, they broke into the house and kidnapped her, demanding a huge ransom for her release. Furthermore, two women surnamed Wang, an aunt and a daughter-in-law, were kidnapped in Changbang, and a ransom of 5,000 yuan was demanded, but an agreement has not yet been reached.

Hangzhou 64

Highway Bureau Purchases Rice to Aid Road Workers: Chen Ticheng, Director of the Provincial Highway Bureau, stated that the road workers on the Hangchang and other roads lacked food, and yesterday specifically requested the Construction Department to forward a request to the provincial government for permission to purchase and transport 3,000 shi of Anhui rice for relief.

Bandits from Changxing Flee to Anji: The Zhejiang Provincial Government received a telegram from Anji County Magistrate Zhang Songnian stating that over 2,000 sword-wielding bandits, after being severely suppressed by the military and police in Si'an, were detouring south through Meixi and eyeing Anji. In addition to declaring martial law and deploying defenses, the county town's military strength was weak. He requested that a large army be quickly dispatched to suppress them. It is reported that the Central Training Corps has been ordered to rush to assist in the suppression.

Opening of the Hangzhou County National Goods Exhibition: The Hangzhou County National Goods Mobile Exhibition opened yesterday (the 19th) at 2:00 PM. Over 800 representatives from various agencies and groups, including Shao Ji, Lu Xingzhuang, and Zhang Baoshan, attended. The chairman reported on the preparations, stating that the Hangzhou County National Goods Promotion Committee planned to convene a mobile exhibition of national goods factories in Hangzhou in order to promote national goods. It was decided that the county government and the county party headquarters would actively prepare. Subsequently, Shao Ji, former Director of the Construction Bureau of Hangzhou County, Lu Xingzhuang, Chairman of the Shanghai National Goods Factory Union, Jiang Senyu, representative of the National Goods Cigarette Maintenance Association, and others delivered speeches before dispersing.

Shaoxing 65

Preventing Bandit Disturbances: Shaoxing rice prices are soaring repeatedly at this time of year when the new harvest is not yet available, making life difficult for the people. In addition to ordering villages to raise funds and handle price stabilization, County Magistrate Tang is deeply concerned that unscrupulous individuals in the mountain villages will take advantage of the situation to create disturbances related to security. Yesterday, he specifically ordered the Public Security Bureau to dispatch troops to be stationed near Kezhen and other mountain villages in order to suppress them. He also dispatched another team to patrol the mountain areas with the Keqiao Public Security Bureau to avoid any accidents, as Keqiao is an important town on the western route.

Xiaoshan 66

Farmers in Sanjiang Township Robbed: The family of Tong Yonggui, a farmer in Sanjiang Township, Xiaoshao, had some savings. On the 17th, in the middle of the night, several bandits suddenly came with flashlights and pistols, broke down the door, and ransacked the house. They looted all the cash, clothing, and other valuables, estimated to be worth over 400 taels of silver.

Rice Prices Continue to Rise: Xiaoshan rice prices have been rising repeatedly recently due to the disappearance of sources and the scarcity of inventory. It is reported that on the 17th, the price of all kinds of white rice rose by another 20 cents. Three-grade white late white xián rice cost 17.2 yuan, and two-grade cost 17 yuan. Furthermore, both grades were reduced to second-class. Three-grade rice is not as good as the previous two-grade rice. Lower grades are available in name only but not in reality. With such expensive rice during a famine year, how will the common people make a living?

Provincial Order to Investigate Village Boundary Dispute: The Ren Sheng Village Committee in the northern part of Xiaoshan and the Eastern Township Autonomous Association are disputing the tax land around Shengwei. They have repeatedly filed complaints with the county government. The county government has ordered the committees to provide detailed reports on the actual situation in order to make a determination. However, the Ren Sheng Village has ignored this order for months. The Department of Civil Affairs has now ordered the county government to investigate and handle the matter quickly. After receiving the order, the county government immediately ordered the committee to determine whether the sandy land of Cai Shuikui and Lu Zhongyue is located on the eastern side of Cuiwei Youshou Stone Mouth, which is a boundary line directly from the northeast two-township border, or on the western side of the boundary line. A detailed report must be submitted within three days without delay.

Sixth Day of the National Education Conference 67

Yesterday, the conference was in recess... Visiting the Mausoleum, Sightseeing, and Banquet

This afternoon... Opening the Fourth General Meeting

The Second National Education Conference was on its sixth day yesterday, Sunday, which was a day of recess. There were visits to mausoleums, sightseeing, and banquets. The situation is recorded below.

Visiting the Mausoleum and Sightseeing 68

▲ Solemn Ceremony to Visit the Remains

▲ Sightseeing at Ancient Temples and Scenic Spots

Yesterday was Sunday, and the conference was in recess. At 9:00 AM, the Reception Section prepared fifteen cars to take the members to visit the Mausoleum of the Premier. Prior to this, the Ministry of Education had specially produced silver-shielded wreaths in Shanghai to be respectfully presented when visiting the Mausoleum. At around 9:00 AM, the members took the cars and departed. At 9:40 AM, they arrived at the Mausoleum. Among those who participated in the visit were members of the conference, including Jin Zengcheng, Zhu Jingnong, Wang Maozu, and Meng Xiancheng, as well as ninety staff members from the two sections of the conference's reception affairs. At 10:30 AM, Jin Zengcheng, as chairman, presided over the ceremony to respectfully visit the Premier's Mausoleum. (1) Everyone stood in silence. (2) Three bows in salute. (3) The chief celebrant respectfully offered the wreath. (4) Three minutes of silence. (5) Everyone filed into the tomb to pay respects. (6) Ceremony completed. Afterwards, the Premier's Mausoleum Management Committee specially opened the tomb chamber. The members queued up and entered the chamber to pay respects. The Premier's coffin was placed in a circular tomb chamber inside the Premier's mausoleum. The coffin was made of white marble and had a full-body sculpture of the Premier's remains on top. A wreath presented by Sun Ke was placed in front of the tomb chamber. The members entered the chamber and paid their respects. After the visit, they filed out. A reporter from this newspaper took a group photo of all the visiting members and staff in front of the memorial hall. After the photo was taken, the members took cars to the invitation of the Yizu School and visited the school. Zhang Shengyi, the director of school affairs, prepared tea and snacks for the reception. After the visit, the members went to Linggu Temple for sightseeing. The temple is an ancient temple from the Southern Dynasty, with dense ancient trees and secluded scenery. The peonies in the temple were in full bloom. Many members carried cameras and took photos inside and outside the temple. At noon, the Ministry of Education prepared a vegetarian meal for the members at the temple.

Welcome Meeting at Yizu School in the Morning 69

▲ Speeches from All Sides Hope to Continue the Legacy of the Martyrs

At 10:30 AM on the 20th, all the teachers and students of the Yizu School held a meeting in the auditorium to welcome the members of the conference. Jin Zengcheng took the stage to give a speech, stating that it was a great honor to visit the school during the holiday. The term "Yizu" (orphans of martyrs) is thought-provoking, making people remember the martyrs. The martyrs sacrificed themselves for the Three Principles of the People and the National Revolution. In the Premier's will, the phrase "to seek freedom and equality for China" has not yet been realized because of the collusion between warlords and imperialism, which has created obstacles and caused the martyrs to fail. It is regrettable. You are the children of revolutionary predecessors. You should emulate the great achievements of your fathers and brothers who sacrificed themselves for the National Revolution, carry on the legacy of your ancestors, and strive for knowledge and revolution. Then, Huang Shiheng, Director of the Education Department of Hunan Province, gave a speech, stating that we have what we have today because of the martyrs. He hopes that the children of the martyrs will receive the most perfect education, so that the seeds of revolution can continue the glory of the martyrs and not let down the hard work of the martyrs. Wu Jiaxiang said that Directors Jin and Huang, one from Guangdong and one from Hunan, are both from the birthplace of the revolution. What they said are all true words. The north is closed and there is nothing worth mentioning. I hope that you will emulate and continue the legacy, so that the destruction of today can be replaced by the success of construction. Finally, Zhang Shengyi, director of school affairs, reported that there are currently 308 students and more than 80 students who have registered but have not been admitted. Because it is the beginning of the school, the equipment and resources need to be expanded but that requires expenses. Although 450,000 yuan has been raised, the money has not been fully collected, so the school affairs have not been able to actively expand according to the plan.

Reception at Jing City Schools in the Afternoon 70

After taking their seats, Gu Shusen, Director of the Municipal Education Bureau, gave a speech, stating that the education situation in Jing City can be divided into two aspects: quantity and quality. In terms of quantity, there are more than 60,000 school-age children in the city, and more than 50,000 children who are out of school. In addition to the more than 13,000 people who have not been admitted, the promotion of compulsory education is imperative. Nanjing is the capital, and its image is at stake. He hopes that the members will focus their efforts and promote its realization. In terms of quality, although there are five experimental primary schools that are experimenting with new educational methods, the economic equipment is difficult to achieve the ideal goal, and it also relies on the members' supervision. Jiang Zexuan was publicly elected by the members to give a reply, stating that today they came for leisure and enjoyed a short rest. He was also pleased to meet comrades from the city's education community at the same time. Director Gu is an expert in vocational education, and he will definitely be able to promote the improvement of education and align it with the purpose of construction. The director is also an educator in rural education. Today, rural education is a top priority. I know that Director Gu will definitely be able to contribute his strengths to set an example for the whole country. In the past, the malpractice of education was to imitate foreigners. Now, starting from experimentation is in line with the national conditions. The capital has five experimental primary schools, and there are also various gatherings every week. I know that the progress of primary school education in Jing City is just beginning. It is a pity that time is tight and I cannot visit all the schools. If we can find a method that is suitable for the national conditions in the future, please enlighten us. The meeting adjourned at 6:00.

Members Take Photo

▲ Hu Hanmin (Guanghua)

four sections on public morality, six sections on hygiene, six sections on attitude, five sections on language, five sections on emotional interests, and three sections on social interaction. These ten sections are weighted as follows: diligence in study accounts for 20 points, thought for 20 points, service for 20 points, discipline for 20 points, public morality for 15 points, hygiene for 15 points, attitude for 10 points, language, emotional interests, and social interaction each for 10 points. The total score for the ten sections is 150 points, with 90 or 100 points considered a passing grade.

Reading the Teacher Training Program (2) "Difference" 81

The success or failure of the teacher training program has a significant impact on the future of compulsory education. During this Second Education Conference, the majority of members considered the teacher funding and resources components of the compulsory education program very important and felt that a detailed discussion was necessary. Mr. Wei Tingsheng, Mr. Jiang Menglin, and others believe that the teacher issue is even more difficult to solve than the funding issue. These insightful remarks are very perceptive. Minister Jiang also pointed out that according to educational statistics from Zhejiang Province, even if all junior high school graduates received teacher training, it would still not be enough. From these results, we can infer that the difficulties in culturally backward provinces and regions are far greater than those in culturally developed Zhejiang. Therefore, the issue of teachers is something that we must pay attention to. During this conference, the desire for the widespread implementation of compulsory education on the one hand, and the failure to promote teacher training in many ways on the other, are truly concerning. It has been the custom in China since the late Qing Dynasty to provide free meals to normal school students. Children from poor but excellent families have been able to attend school, and as a result, many excellent people have become elementary school teachers, dedicating themselves to the cause of primary education in our country with remarkable results that are evident to all. In the current plan, the system of providing free meals has been abolished, and it is deeply feared that this will cause great panic in normal schools across the country in future student recruitment. In Zhejiang, few students enroll due to the collection of meal fees. In Jiangsu, the number of candidates increased significantly after the normal school program switched from collecting meal fees to providing free meals. All of these facts prove that normal school students should not be charged meal fees. Furthermore, if we want to achieve universal education in the future, we must focus on rural areas, and the training of teachers should particularly emphasize farmers' children. In our country, where the national economy is weak, how can the average farmer afford the cost of their children's meals, books, and supplies at normal school? Therefore, we must either abandon the idea of universal education in our country altogether, or if we want to achieve it, the first problem to be solved must be the issue of free meals. If national finances make it difficult to bear this significant expense, then at the very least, we must maintain the excellent system of not collecting meal fees for training elementary school teachers. It is my sincere hope that the members of the conference and government authorities will give this careful consideration.

Summary of Proposals (3) 82

▲ Plan to Improve and Develop Overseas Chinese Education (Continued)

4. The construction and equipment of overseas Chinese schools should follow the standards and methods set by the Ministry of Education, but may refer to the standards set by local governments.

5. Supplementary items for moral education in overseas Chinese schools: Each year, month, and week's moral education activities should be determined locally and submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval.

6. Overseas Chinese school curriculum and teaching materials: (1) The curriculum should be compiled locally according to the standards promulgated by the Ministry of Education. (2) Textbooks and teaching materials should be reviewed according to the review methods set by the Ministry of Education. Existing applicable versions should be approved or rewarded, and standards should be set to allow private individuals to edit, review, and publish them, with rewards given to the best. (3) Special teaching materials should be commissioned by the Ministry of Education to be edited by experts. (4) For the adoption of foreign textbooks, local committees should select, review, and revise them. (5) Teaching aids and experiments should be the same as those used in domestic schools.

7. Overseas Chinese school teachers: (1) Reorganize domestic institutions for training teachers for overseas Chinese schools, establish normal schools at home and abroad, or subsidize overseas high schools and normal schools to commission the training of teachers. (2) Register teachers: overseas registration is handled by consulates, domestic registration is handled by local education administrative agencies in Nanjing, Shanghai, Guangzhou, Xiamen, and Shantou. The methods include checking academic performance or conducting appropriate examinations. Current teachers should be treated more leniently, while those wishing to teach in the future should be treated strictly. Qualified teachers should be given permits. (3) Teachers with misconduct should have their permits revoked or be dismissed, or be disciplined after returning to the country. (4) The Ministry of Education should order education authorities in Nanjing, Shanghai, Guangzhou, Xiamen, Shantou, and other places to organize teacher introduction agencies to handle introduction matters. (5) The Ministry of Education should set several standards for salary standards and seniority-based salary increase methods. (6) The Ministry of Education should set rewards and protection measures, give bonuses to outstanding teachers, supplement outstanding domestic teachers to work overseas, and ensure that teachers are not dismissed without reason. Teachers hired to return to the country should have a contract of at least two years, and their salaries should be calculated for twelve months. Travel expenses and accommodation should be provided by the school. (7) Advanced training methods should be the same as for domestic teachers.

8. Overseas Chinese school students: (1) Overseas Chinese schools should set up free places. (2) The Ministry of Education should set up methods for overseas Chinese students to return to the country for further education, determine quotas, and provide financial assistance. (3) Overseas consulates and education associations should handle guidance for further education. The Ministry of Education should order educational advisors in Shanghai, Guangzhou, Shantou, Xiamen, and Tianjin to guide further education.

9. Guidance system: (1) Consulate specialists must have graduated from high school or above with normal school training and have more than five years of educational experience. They must be proficient in the national language and a foreign language, have good character and health, understand the principles of the party, and be familiar with overseas Chinese affairs. (2) Each region should be divided into several guidance areas, with one or two schools designated as the center of each area to organize guidance meetings and plan guidance and improvement measures. The central school should also organize research associations with other schools to study education. (3) The Ministry of Education should regularly send personnel to inspect and guide.

(VII) Social Education

1. Supplementary Education: (1) Institutions: half-day schools, literacy night schools, holiday supplementary schools, women's supplementary schools. (2) Curriculum: general academic subjects and vocational subjects should be determined by consulates and education specialists. (3) Regulations should be promulgated by the Ministry of Education.

2. Social Education: (1) Institutions: popular libraries, reading rooms, popular lecture halls, new drama performances, clubs, and family improvement associations. (2) Guidance: Education Associations. (3) Funding: self-raised or granted subsidies.

3. Temporary Gatherings: (1) Promotion of sports, hygiene, the national language, encouraging learning, women's liberation, and family improvement. (2) Organizers: Education Associations, etc.

4. Various undertakings are mostly jointly organized by overseas Chinese education groups.

▲ Plan to Improve Social Education

(I) General Outline

1. Principles: A. The administrative organization should be simple. B. Implementing agencies should be centralized. C. Implementation procedures should be experimental first and then promoted. D. Implementing personnel should be specially trained. E. Funding should be generous and its independence should be guaranteed. F. The government should guide society to promote it with all its might.

2. Administrative Organization (in addition to the Department or Section of Social Education already established by the Ministry of Education and the Provincial Departments of Education): (1) The municipal and county education bureaus should set up a Social Education Section or Division. (2) Competent authorities at all levels may organize design or research committees.

3. Implementing Agencies: A. Ordinary: public education centers, libraries, museums, art galleries, gymnasiums, sports fields, public and agricultural/industrial/commercial supplementary schools, etc. B. Special: institutions for the disabled, reformatories, revolutionary museums, etc., with public education centers serving as the center for implementation and experimentation.

4. Implementation Procedures: First establish an experimental agency, and after obtaining effective implementation methods and successfully training implementing personnel, then add more in stages.

5. Personnel Training: (1) Provide various social education implementing agencies with a large number of working personnel. (2) Provide social education research experiments and cultivate personnel with higher academic knowledge. The former personnel should be developed separately in various teacher training institutions at all levels, or trained in the experimental social education center.

6. Funding Methods: A. The central government has previously clearly stipulated that social education

Education administrative agencies should strictly abide by it. B. In wealthy areas, the proportion of funding should be increased from 20% to 30%. C. For large-scale social education projects, the central, provincial, and county governments should allocate special funds as start-up costs or foundations. D. Each time the central or local government raises various public bonds, 10% to 20% of the proceeds should be allocated to social education funding.

7. Other matters should be coordinated with all government agencies and promoted with all efforts.

(II) Agricultural/Industrial/Commercial Vocational Supplementary Education

1. Principles: A. Provide vocational training to adults who have received national literacy education or have some literacy skills, supplementing the knowledge and skills necessary for their lives and occupations. B. For those who have received national literacy training

Experience, emphasize literacy training. C. In addition to paying attention to vocational training, also provide national training, health education, beautification, public entertainment, and moral improvement education. D. The types should be divided into industrial, commercial, agricultural, domestic, and other vocational supplementary education. E. It should be held after the completion of national literacy training, or it can be held simultaneously with other programs. First start with trial programs in urban industrial and commercial developed areas or densely populated villages, and gradually expand to remote rural areas to run small-scale agricultural supplementary schools. F. The age of the educated should range from twelve to fifty years old. G. The organization and structure should be flexible and adapted to local conditions.

2. Types: A. General advanced public supplementary schools: (1) Advanced public schools. (2) Advanced youth supplementary schools. B. Vocational supplementary schools.

3. Structure, Subjects, and Time: A. The structure should be divided into semester system and subject system. The semester system requires the completion of several semesters to graduate. Subjects

The Scout Performance Yesterday

(Photo by Nanjing Guanghua)

system requires the completion of certain subjects to graduate. B. The class time of vocational supplementary schools should take advantage of the learners' spare time from work, or open night classes, or open Sunday classes, or during farm breaks.

4. Administrative Essentials: A. The provincial, municipal, and county education administrative agencies are responsible for directing, supervising, promoting, and expanding, and for guiding improvement. B. The administrative agencies should contact various local educational institutions and vocational groups, and should appropriately establish vocational guidance centers and vocational introduction departments. C. All local public groups, schools, factories, stores, or other groups have the responsibility to concurrently run vocational supplementary schools. D. Industrial and commercial supplementary schools should supervise factories and stores to cooperate in running schools according to the Outline of Workers' Education Plan. E. Agricultural supplementary schools should be jointly run by the Agricultural Extension Committee and agricultural instructors according to the Agricultural Extension Regulations. F. Domestic and women's vocational supplementary schools should be jointly run by women's associations and other women's groups.

5. Teacher Training Methods: Carefully plan and establish teacher training institutions of all levels and types.

6. School Buildings and Equipment: A. In addition to borrowing existing schools, temples, and guild halls, industrial and commercial supplementary schools should utilize the conference rooms and reception rooms of factories and stores as classrooms, and utilize existing equipment for practical training. B. In addition to borrowing existing agricultural extension and agricultural experimental institutions, temples, and guild halls, agricultural and domestic supplementary schools should also utilize existing houses and equipment of rural normal schools, rural elementary schools, cooperative institutions, and other groups.

7. Funding: Use the original national literacy training fees to continue to run agricultural/industrial/commercial vocational supplementary education.

(III) Plan and Promote Various Social

Education Main Institutions

First Term of Tutelage Begins (Four Years) (1) The central government should establish a public theater in the capital, with an attached actor training institute and a music training institute. The start-up cost is 400,000 yuan, and the annual operating cost is 100,000 yuan. (2) Add drama and music departments or drama and music lectures to the colleges of education or liberal arts colleges of national universities. (3) The public drama actor training institute, music training institute, and drama or music departments of universities should organize new drama troupes and music groups to perform in various places, depending on economic conditions. (4) The Ministry of Education, together with the drama or music departments of universities, should select lyrics, tunes, scripts, etc., and entrust the gramophone company to record and play them. The central government allocates 100,000 yuan per year for the use of items (3) and (4). (5) The public theater should set up an educational film production institute (including an actor training institute) to produce educational films. The start-up cost is 600,000 yuan, and the annual operating cost is 150,000 yuan. (6) The public theater should set up a broadcast radio station. The start-up cost is 80,000 yuan, and the annual operating cost is 20,000 yuan. (7) Each province or special municipality should refer to the above methods and gradually raise funds to establish provincial theaters, actor training institutes, broadcast radio stations, etc. Public education centers in each city and county should install radios as much as possible. It would be even better if relay stations could be set up and radios could be installed in public tea gardens and rural social centers.

3. Second Term (Years 5-8) (1) The central government should establish a public sports field in the capital, with a start-up cost of approximately 120,000 yuan and an operating cost of

Investigate the actual situation of sports fields in each county and find ways to supervise, improve, and promote them. (3) Each town and village should make full use of school sports fields and their equipment for public use. (4) The Ministry of Education should formulate standards for the equipment of various sports fields. The provincial departments of education should formulate various detailed rules for the equipment of sports fields based on the standards for selection by various cities and counties. (5) Educational administrative agencies at all levels should appropriately set up physical education instructors. (6) Teacher training institutions at all levels should appropriately train physical education instructors. (7) When implementing adult supplementary education, whether it is national literacy training or vocational supplementary education, physical education should be incorporated within the possible scope. (8) The Ministry of Education, together with the Ministry of Health, should formulate and promulgate methods for improving physical fitness. (9) The educational administrative agencies should promote three types of physical education: A. Each province, city, and county should hold a large-scale public sports meeting once a year or every two years. B. Local educational administrative agencies and public sports fields should hold health competitions and children's competitions once each year or every two years. C. At various events, educational administrative agencies and public sports fields should hold special recreational sports meetings and conduct physical education promotion.

Three, the third phase (the ninth to twelfth year) (1) The central government shall raise funds to establish public libraries in the capital, with a start-up cost of approximately 400,000 yuan and an annual operating cost of approximately 100,000 yuan. (2) The Ministry of Education shall investigate the libraries in each province, city, and county, supervise and improve their promotion, and the libraries in each city and county must establish branch libraries, mobile libraries, circulation points for books and newspapers, and agency offices, and supervise and promote the establishment of those that have not yet been established. (3) Libraries in schools at all levels shall be gradually opened to the public. (4) The Ministry of Education shall formulate equipment and book purchasing standards for various libraries, and the provincial education departments shall formulate equipment details based on the standards, as well as several book purchasing catalogs for selection by various cities and counties. (5) National and provincial universities or established private universities shall appropriately open classes or establish specialized courses to train various library personnel. (6) Various libraries shall make use of the books in their collection to compile popular reading materials and popular publications. (7) Various libraries should investigate and collect public reading materials and forward them to the competent education administrative agency for submission to the Ministry of Education for review.

Four, the fourth phase (the thirteenth to sixteenth year) (1) The central government shall raise funds to establish public museums in the capital, with a start-up cost of approximately 400,000 yuan and an annual operating cost of approximately 100,000 yuan. (2) The central government should continue to properly preserve the documents and antiquities in the Forbidden City, Sanhai, and the Temple of Heaven in Beiping, and vigorously expand them to make them a complete national museum during this period. The expansion cost is approximately 200,000 yuan, and the annual cost is approximately 50,000 yuan. (3) The provinces or special municipalities shall gradually raise funds to establish provincial museums during this period. (4) The public education centers in each city and county should appropriately set up a museum department. (5) The museums and museum departments should solicit ancient artifacts from private collections for display. (6) The museums and museum departments should be responsible for preserving local literature and artifacts. Detailed measures shall be formulated and promulgated by the Ministry of Education in conjunction with the Ministry of Internal Affairs. (7) Research institutes and university research institutes shall organize artifact investigation teams to investigate artifacts and monuments, and excavate artifacts and other items related to literature and artifacts. Detailed measures shall be formulated and promulgated by the Ministry of Education in conjunction with the Ministry of Internal Affairs.

Five, the fifth phase (the seventeenth to twentieth year) (1) The central government should raise funds to establish public art galleries in the capital, with a start-up cost of approximately 400,000 yuan and an annual operating cost of approximately 100,000 yuan. (2) Divide the art section of the Forbidden City, Sanhai, and the Temple of Heaven in Beiping and vigorously expand it to make it a complete national art gallery during this period. The start-up cost is approximately 200,000 yuan, and the annual operating cost is approximately 50,000 yuan. (3) Starting from this period, the central government should allocate 20,000 yuan annually to reward art and hold exhibitions. The reward methods and exhibition methods shall be formulated and promulgated by the Ministry of Education. (4) The provinces or special municipalities should raise funds to establish art galleries during this period. (5) The public education centers in each city and county should increase the art department as much as possible within the possible scope. (6) The art galleries and art departments should seek private collections or works for display.

(4) Prepare Special Education and Reformatory Education

1. Educational institutions for children or young people with disabilities should be provincial in principle. Each province should first run a trial, and then promote it to various cities and counties. The funds shall be appropriated from the original general education funds of each province. The curriculum, teaching, and training methods shall be formulated by the education departments of each province and submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval.

2. The reformatory education of criminals shall be conducted by the education departments of each province in conjunction with the Xiao-Zhong Court, first in the provincial capital prison, and then promoted to various cities and counties. The funds shall be provided from the judicial expenses.

3. The Testing and Research Department of the Ministry of Education should test the psychology of criminals, and then organize a Reformatory Education Class Research Committee to formulate curriculum standards, promulgate them for trial implementation, and then revise them based on the results of the trial. The curriculum content should emphasize both national literacy training and vocational training. The education departments of each province shall formulate detailed curricula based on the standards and submit them to the Ministry of Education for approval.

(5) Changing Customs and Promoting Public Entertainment

1. Negative Aspects: A. Register the names, types, addresses, number of performers, names, education level, and names of performed scripts, films, songs, etc. of the agencies engaged in this type of occupation. B. Train performers for a period of four to six months, which shall be organized by the municipal education administrative agency with a cost of approximately 1,000 yuan per period. C. Those that have not been reviewed shall be reviewed by the municipal and county Entertainment Business Review Committees. D. Distinguish between good and bad, and give permission, improvement, and prohibition punishments.

2. Positive Aspects: A. Completely preserve the old entertainment that does not need to be changed, such as New Year's parades, singing, drums and music, music, chess, martial arts, walking, racing, swimming, kites, Jianzi, etc. B. Old entertainment that can still be preserved after improvement, such as performing dramas, large drums, storytelling, mountain songs, ditties, etc. C. New entertainment that should be promoted, such as various new chess games, various ball games, new dramas, lantern slides, gramophones, costume speeches, film competitions, clubs, parent-teacher meetings, variety shows, and dinners.

3. Each city and county may appropriately establish a Promotion Committee. The organizational law of the committee shall be formulated by each city and county and submitted to the Education Department for implementation.

4. Each city and county may appropriately establish public tea gardens, public entertainment fields, large drum storytelling fields, film fields, etc., and may encourage commercial operations, provide guidance, and restrict ticket prices to achieve parity.

5. Each city and county should give prizes, bonuses, and other rewards for various entertainment.

(6) Cooperative Measures for Social Education and School Education

1. School staff and equipment should be used as much as possible as the center for promoting social education.

2. In running public education, rural normal schools and rural primary schools should be used as the center.

3. High schools and above should seek to promote the development of education in popular science and other aspects.

4. School libraries and reading rooms should be opened appropriately.

5. In places where there are no museums, schools should open specimen rooms appropriately.

6. All levels of schools must make public speeches, performances, variety shows, etc.

7. Schools at all levels should give popular lectures to the public on a regular basis.

8. Places with libraries, museums, gymnasiums, etc. should do their best to facilitate local students to visit, read, experiment, and exercise.
